  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_179e7982-b093-4f32-8508-32fbff0a7650'

<span id="freeTextContainer12273931868901962631">Lorna, Jennifer and Seth struggle to reach the Hive amid the chaos of Armageddon. Their bodies and minds wasted, will Lorna survive long enough to rat out Seth's psychotic cruelty?   <span id="freeText12273931868901962631" style="display:none">Lorna, Jennifer and Seth struggle to reach the Hive amid the chaos of Armageddon. Their bodies and minds wasted, will Lorna survive long enough to rat out Seth's psychotic cruelty? And what of the innocent child Suzy that has been kidnapped by Doc Benjamin's tribe of female enslaving barbarians? What fate awaits the beloved planet Earth?<br /><br />The Hive is now one big happy family, romance is in the air as our survivors become mysteriously fit and robust, pheromones and testosterone fly as all accept the new law of the Hive: protect the animals at all cost.<br /><br />Netty, Wil and Baby now hold the power with the help of the terrifying Kreyven. Shock after shock ensues as the survivors unravel most of the mysteries of the Hive and mourn unexpected deaths. The overriding surprise will be a complete blast from Netty's past, tying up all of the unanswered questions from Baby.</span>

<div id="review_708261406" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/708261406" />
    <a title="Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6665735-books"><img alt="Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1419956881p2/6665735.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/708261406?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Books" href="/user/show/6665735-books">Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6665735-books?shelf=reviewed-2013">reviewed-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer708261406" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4919339623835973420">After finishing the fourth book in this magnificent series, I couldn’t wait for the release of the fifth, titled “Evil Among Us”. With each new release in the Species Intervention #6609 Series, my expectations keep getting higher, and as yet Accinni has not let me down. In “Evil Among Us” the suspense and intrigue builds up to breaking point and seeing as this is the second to last book in this series, I was riveted. <br/><br/>In keeping with the previous four books, plot twists and secrets are plentiful,</span>
  <span id="freeText4919339623835973420" style="display:none">After finishing the fourth book in this magnificent series, I couldn’t wait for the release of the fifth, titled “Evil Among Us”. With each new release in the Species Intervention #6609 Series, my expectations keep getting higher, and as yet Accinni has not let me down. In “Evil Among Us” the suspense and intrigue builds up to breaking point and seeing as this is the second to last book in this series, I was riveted. <br /><br />In keeping with the previous four books, plot twists and secrets are plentiful, although there are also several revelations. The events in this book didn’t shock me as much as some of the happenings in the previous books, but one specific character (who thankfully takes his last breath in this installment) still managed to terrify me with his presence and his strife-causing doings. It’s hard for me to imagine such evil human beings exist, but I’ve come to believe that in this day and age anything is possible. Even more so, I imagine, when chaos reigns. The Hive is certainly an interesting place to be. I was surprised at some of the reactions to certain actions, and though I was left with more questions, I’ll try to be patient while anxiously awaiting the conclusion to this hard-hitting series.<br /><br />If science fiction and dystopian are your genres of choice, and if conservation is something you feel strongly about, you definitely need to get these books. This entire series (the books I’ve read so far), is written with clever insight into the dark side of human nature and the extent of greed, but also focuses on the individuals making sacrifices for the greater good. Accinni’s involvement in supporting the preservation of wildlife shows that she not only writes about what is important to her (and what should be important to all of us in preserving our heritage), but her participation in efforts to conserve proves that she is serious about the subject matter of her books. Though most of what she writes is fictional, the truths of our destructive nature cannot be ignored. For a highly intelligent read that gets you thinking, start with the first book and see why this is fast becoming such a popular series!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4919339623835973420" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_621666652" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/621666652" />
    <a title="Wanda Hartzenberg" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5663614-wanda-hartzenberg"><img alt="Wanda Hartzenberg" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442880312p2/5663614.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/621666652?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wanda Hartzenberg" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wanda Hartzenberg" href="/user/show/5663614-wanda-hartzenberg">Wanda Hartzenberg</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5663614-wanda-hartzenberg?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer621666652" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15179433707810730529">Evil Among Us [Book 5 in the Species intervention series]<br/>This has been an amazing series and in this the penultimate book in the series some secrets have been revealed to the reader.<br/>Baby and Echo have indeed been up to no good. But you will need to read it for yourself to see what they have been up to.<br/>Seth …..What to say about him. The dark side in me would have made his end gorier but I did not write the book so I had to be content with his death.<br/>Kenya is still pregnant and herein lies my probl</span>
  <span id="freeText15179433707810730529" style="display:none">Evil Among Us [Book 5 in the Species intervention series]<br />This has been an amazing series and in this the penultimate book in the series some secrets have been revealed to the reader.<br />Baby and Echo have indeed been up to no good. But you will need to read it for yourself to see what they have been up to.<br />Seth …..What to say about him. The dark side in me would have made his end gorier but I did not write the book so I had to be content with his death.<br />Kenya is still pregnant and herein lies my problem with the logic of the narrative, I followed it nicely where it was explained why Kenya will remain pregnant as long as she is in the hive. Then I remembered the piglets…thank you Seth!!! And three elephants fell pregnant and birthed…. hmmm. So now I no longer understand the logic and how it is valid for one species but not for the other.<br />In this book the author really, really pushes the envelope against the human race and were I not too such a large degree in agreement with her regarding our continual negative impact I think I might have started to take offence at some stage during this book. My love for animals saved me from this judgment although it did cross my mind that it might be hard for others to follow. That however will only be an issue if the reader has not read the series in sequence. <br />The strife that Seth causes and the residual effects of his poison within the Hive was expertly done by the author as character's goes Seth is a guy I loved to hate…. and I mean Hate. Even after his death the Hive is still in upset and it worked perfectly to show how one evil influence affects everything even after it has been removed. I loved this part of the story. <br />Nettie … hmm her reaction to what Baby and Echo did shocked me. I am unsure as to why. It was very human and very understandable but I had come to believe that she and Will together with some of the other elders have moved on and ascended to a higher state of being. If I were in the Hive I would not have been so easy to accept her action and I would have been very weary of somebody with this much power still being ruled by her emotions.<br /><br />All in all a great fast read. I would ideally give it a 4.5 star rating but since it is not an option I will go with a 5*. <br />WaAr</span>

    <a title="Fenny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10519901-fenny"><img alt="Fenny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364760010p2/10519901.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/624332285?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fenny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fenny" href="/user/show/10519901-fenny">Fenny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer624332285" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12309647385652130812">The fifth in the Species Intervention #6609 Series is a heart wrenching story of the evil nature incarnate. Again J.K. Accinni has presented us with a skillful written tale where the characters gain even more depth as we follow them on their journey of adaptation to life inside the Hive.<br/><br/>The Hive is a good place to be, it provides for all the needs of its inhabitants, first and foremost the animals, but the humans are certainly not forgotten. As the people adjust to their new life good ánd strang</span>
  <span id="freeText12309647385652130812" style="display:none">The fifth in the Species Intervention #6609 Series is a heart wrenching story of the evil nature incarnate. Again J.K. Accinni has presented us with a skillful written tale where the characters gain even more depth as we follow them on their journey of adaptation to life inside the Hive.<br /><br />The Hive is a good place to be, it provides for all the needs of its inhabitants, first and foremost the animals, but the humans are certainly not forgotten. As the people adjust to their new life good ánd strange things happen. A number of questions raised from the previous books are answered, but at the same time several other points raise new ones.<br /><br />Relationship develop, creating all sorts of tension and jealousy. When Seth, Lorna and a fox tumble into the Hive and the fox’ mate as well as Jennifer is found just outside the entrance – tension increases and emotions run high. <br /><br />The title is very apt as a lot of evil things happen not only on earth but also in the Hive, that supposedly safe haven. It is unimaginable that the Elders can be deceived or that the Womb allows them to be fooled. Yet... <br /><br />The fairy tale aspect of the Hive is mostly gone – lost in the unspeakable and unthinkable actions and dire consequences that take place, culminating in the loss of animal and human life.<br /><br />Most shockingly, however is the secret that Baby and Echo harbour. Not only that, the response of Netty in particular will raise some eyebrows as it did mine. <br /><br />As evil is repaid with evil – something I didn’t see coming – there still is redemption if the right choice is made and forgiveness is sought.<br /><br />As new mysteries appear pertaining the future of life after the Hive and with no clarity yet as far as Scotty being The One, I am impatiently waiting for the next book to come out to find out how the whole story will be wrapped up. Having come to know J.K. Accinni, no doubt it will be beautifully written and constructed with a few surprises thrown in!<br /><br />P.S. And for the insiders: my favourite part is about the cake!</span>

<div id="review_693987974" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/693987974" />
    <a title="Lynn Worton" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7917492-lynn-worton"><img alt="Lynn Worton" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435527343p2/7917492.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/693987974?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lynn Worton" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lynn Worton" href="/user/show/7917492-lynn-worton">Lynn Worton</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer693987974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9459376040160533876">This is the fifth book in an amazing series! I loved it!<br/><br/>In the aftermath of the terrorist attack, Lorna, Jennifer and Seth are struggling to reach the Hive. They face several obstacles along the way. Meanwhile, inside the Hive, life has settled down somewhat, and Abby, Scotty, Jose, Echo, Chloe, along with Captain Cobby and his son, Kane, Peter, Ginger Mae, her daughter Daisy, Kenya, Johno, Netty, Wil and Baby, are gifted the protection of the Womb.<br/><br/>I found this story not as dark as the previous </span>
  <span id="freeText9459376040160533876" style="display:none">This is the fifth book in an amazing series! I loved it!<br /><br />In the aftermath of the terrorist attack, Lorna, Jennifer and Seth are struggling to reach the Hive. They face several obstacles along the way. Meanwhile, inside the Hive, life has settled down somewhat, and Abby, Scotty, Jose, Echo, Chloe, along with Captain Cobby and his son, Kane, Peter, Ginger Mae, her daughter Daisy, Kenya, Johno, Netty, Wil and Baby, are gifted the protection of the Womb.<br /><br />I found this story not as dark as the previous four books, but even so, this book has so many twists and turns I struggled to put it down! There are several revelations that shocked me, but I also found myself faced with several new questions. Such as, "What is the purpose of the Womb's delaying the birth of Kenya's baby?" and "What will the future hold for the survivors?". I am hoping that these and other questions will be answered in the sixth book, which I am now looking forward to reading! *SPOILER ALERT* I don't normally write spoilers, but in this case I have to! - I must admit that I was not sad to read about Seth's demise! He was a REALLY nasty piece of work!<br /><br />On a side note: I hope that humanity will avoid anything like a nuclear war. We are the only sentient beings (that I know of!) on this planet that is causing damage to it. I am not surprised that Mother Nature is fighting back: Earthquakes, Tsunami's, Hurricanes etc. I sometimes feel that we are reaping the cosmic Karma caused by our actions and greed!<br /><br />J.K. Accinni is a fantastic writer and has become one of my favourite authors. Her stories are most certainly dark, but there is compassion, and a plea to change our ways in her work. I agree with her sentiments. It is not too late, but one day it may be, and there will be no return.<br /><br />I highly recommend this book (and series) if you love Sci-fi or Dystopian genres. - Lynn Worton</span>
  <a data-text-id="9459376040160533876" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText10810649813986197110" style="display:none">After reading the first four books I had a lot of expectations and this book certainly delivered.<br />It certainly kept you on your toes with Lorna, Seth and Jennifer arriving at the Hive, with only one of them surviving.<br />Then there is the love triangle that is Emma, Kane and Kenya which results in sadness.<br />Then whilst all of the animals are giving birth to babies Kenya is still heavily pregnant after being in the Hive for six months, only to be told that they will all remain in the Hive for a century and things will remain the same, including Kenya's pregnancy. When I read that I thought 'Oh my gosh, poor girl' Nine months is bad enough being pregnant but to be pregnant for over one hundred years? nu uh.<br />Then there is a blast from the past, and not in a good way. What has Baby and Echo been hiding from everyone? I was definitely surprised when I found out.<br />This is definitely a must read and I could see this whole series as a movie!</span>

  <span id="freeText2513024732993653899" style="display:none">This book was even more amazing then the last four books in the series. And they were pretty amazing. My heart felt like it was going to beat out of my chest. At the excitement awaiting on the next page. As the survivors became accustomed to living everyday life within the womb. They have learned to live together as a family. Watching out for one another. Kenya's is 15 months pregnant and needing the most attention. Sharing daily chores to help everything run smooth and ensure the safety of each other and the animals trusted in their care of the hive. All types of relationships begin to form. The womb will provide and the womb does provide. The people notice their health has improved, Everyone believes the grown food is the cause of them looking and feeling much younger. The Elders, Netty and Wil, are holding secrets. They entrust Abby and Jose with the knowledge they hold. Peter brings everyone's attention to a secret, Baby and Echo hold. Some unexpecting guest find their way at the entrance of the hive. The survivors sense a disturbance and send some of the men to go check it out. They find two unrecognizable figures and a very sick fox tangled in the mucus membrane in the entrance of the cavern. Taking what they think is a women and a man, to the healing room of the womb. Soon to find out they invited a killer into their home. That's when deceit and betrayal start to happen amongst them. Trust is tested and relationships get broken. The member were becoming suspicious and wanted answers. Secrets were exposed to the group. Some not willing to except them. But needing life in the womb to slowly return to a calm presence around them. Nothing was challenged. There'll always be secrets between the Elders and the Womb.</span>

<div id="review_622678834" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/622678834" />
    <a title="Gretchen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7428046-gretchen"><img alt="Gretchen" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/622678834?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gretchen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gretchen" href="/user/show/7428046-gretchen">Gretchen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer622678834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14837359157442445684">Evil Among Us is the fifth book in the Species Intervention #6609 series. I was unable to put this one down, causing more sleep deprivation due to J.K. Accinni's brilliant writing.<br/><br/>Living in the hive, the group slowly changes. Their life revolves around each other and the animals. They regain their youth, their health, and become (for the most part) content in their situation. However, all is not what it seems and the rescue of Seth, Lorna, and Jennifer sets off a chain reaction that threatens ev</span>
  <span id="freeText14837359157442445684" style="display:none">Evil Among Us is the fifth book in the Species Intervention #6609 series. I was unable to put this one down, causing more sleep deprivation due to J.K. Accinni's brilliant writing.<br /><br />Living in the hive, the group slowly changes. Their life revolves around each other and the animals. They regain their youth, their health, and become (for the most part) content in their situation. However, all is not what it seems and the rescue of Seth, Lorna, and Jennifer sets off a chain reaction that threatens everyone's safety...<br /><br />Accinni's writing is eerily realistic. Despite being in a sci-fi/fantasy/post-apocalyptic setting, the characters, the reactions, the true "humanity" comes through. I can see this happening. I can see these situations coming up. Unfortunately, this realism is a chilling reminder of the worst that the human race is capable of. This series has actually forced me to deal with a couple of issues that I have been avoiding and that is never comfortable. Yet, as uncomfortable as I may be at times while reading these books, I am caught up in the story. I want to know what happens and it is going to be difficult to wait for the next book, hopefully coming out in August.<br /><br />This is not a children's series, nor, in my opinion, young adult. Due to the violence, unless a teen is very mature, I would recommend it for adult readers only. The violence is necessary to the story line and to character development. It is not crudely done, but it is disturbing, so please be aware of it if you are a sensitive reader.<br /><br />I highly recommend this series.<br /><br />Species Intervention #6609<br />Baby<br />Echo<br />Armageddon Cometh<br />The Hive<br />Evil Among Us<br />and The One, coming soon...</span>
  <a data-text-id="14837359157442445684" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9534934578329341352">Wow! Where do I start with this book? First let me say this cover does look bad ass! I mean right? If you have read the other books you will understand the look of this cover. I have to say I wonder where this author gets her ideas for this series of books, because she has not disappointed me once and I know for sure her books will be added to my small list of books to re-read again later on.<br/><br/>You will fall in love with the characters and with others you will wonder what the heck is wrong with you</span>
  <span id="freeText9534934578329341352" style="display:none">Wow! Where do I start with this book? First let me say this cover does look bad ass! I mean right? If you have read the other books you will understand the look of this cover. I have to say I wonder where this author gets her ideas for this series of books, because she has not disappointed me once and I know for sure her books will be added to my small list of books to re-read again later on.<br /><br />You will fall in love with the characters and with others you will wonder what the heck is wrong with you. Come to your senses man or woman! I do have to say I really would like to know what has happened with Suzy as if you read in the book before this one you know she was kidnapped! So she is no longer with her grandmother or sister anymore. <br /><br />The way the author describes the scenes in such detail has me in aww and amazement along with the shudders and going oh wow what an imagination. <br /><br />My heart literally goes out to Kenya! Poor, poor Kenya and her pregnancy. Let me just say you got this girl. lol. <br /><br />There will be secrets that come to life and so many questions! Echo and Baby have something going on that even those that are close to them do not even know about. <br /><br />Overall this was an amazing book to read, and I kind of didn't want it to end! Because the ending has me wondering what is going on with all the Elders! They have something up their sleeve and I would like to know what that is.<br /><br />I would highly suggest you go out and get this book as it is WONDERFUL! But I would suggest you also read the other books in the series as so you do not get confused and wonder what is going on. <br /></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer630611894" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9135475078751324667">Evil Among Us is the fifth installment to the Species Intervention Series. It picks up six months after the group of survivors has been led into the hive. The survivors have fallen into a routine that is about to be shaken to the core with the arrival of Clyde's wife Lorna, his granddaughter Jennifer, and their sadistic traveling companion Seth. It seems the hive is still not rid of the evil of humanity. We learn that the occupants of the hive will be there for a century while the earth prepares</span>
  <span id="freeText9135475078751324667" style="display:none">Evil Among Us is the fifth installment to the Species Intervention Series. It picks up six months after the group of survivors has been led into the hive. The survivors have fallen into a routine that is about to be shaken to the core with the arrival of Clyde's wife Lorna, his granddaughter Jennifer, and their sadistic traveling companion Seth. It seems the hive is still not rid of the evil of humanity. We learn that the occupants of the hive will be there for a century while the earth prepares itself for the animals return. "How can these human live a century?" you may ask. The answer is the womb! It is making them look younger and feel healthier as they sleep. Poor pregnant Kenya who is six months past due learns that she will not be having her baby until they leave the hive and she is determined to change it. Wil and Netty have some secrets that have been hinted at but not revealed and Baby and Echo have a huge secret of their own! How will these survivors co exist for 100 years? Who will survive until the end?<br /> Accinni did an awesome job on this one. I found this book hard to put down once I started reading it. The characters keep developing and giving me a new dynamic to the story and their lives. Each book is better and better. I can't wait for The One to come out so I can continue my adventure. This is a series that I see myself reading over and over for years to come! BY Amanda F of <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.FaeBooks.co.uk">www.FaeBooks.co.uk</a></span>

  <span id="freeText15526857416259093274" style="display:none">5th book...and best thus far! I tend not to want to give a lot away, so my reviews are more emotion based. I feel like J.K. Accinni is writing with a point, but every character has an amazing co-relation. I was very happy to see some things going on for Baby, and see some connections that were made amongst others, and ....sort of happy about a situation that occurred leading to---someone's fate. I think this book brings the series round and makes things connect, and honestly-I can feel the earthly connection here, almost reading as if some of it we live daily. I don't ever question a genius in the works and JK has certainly attained that level. You read and wonder, is that really possible, how do we not know whats going on, where did that come from? Its a book that is made to bring out more secrets, bring out some truths, and set a precedence in the series. There simply is Evil Among Us, and we never know where or in whom, or through what it may be lurking. ....And now, I am gripping waiting for the next book. <br /><br />This is a series I highly recommend to anyone looking to be captured into a book they will not want to put down. I greatly enjoyed another shockingly surprising book written by the talented J.Kelly Accinni. Thank you JK for sharing your visions, thoughts, and incredible perspectives through your words.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18423716738083482721">Loved it! It took me a little to figure out who was who again as it has been a while between this book and the last, and needless to say I forget things after thirty minutes. However once the characters were well established and I picked up the story again, it completely ran away with me. I started and finished within a couple of hours because I simply could not put it down. I loved how some of the secrets were revealed in Evil Among Us, and I also loved the horror and anticipation that the char</span>
  <span id="freeText18423716738083482721" style="display:none">Loved it! It took me a little to figure out who was who again as it has been a while between this book and the last, and needless to say I forget things after thirty minutes. However once the characters were well established and I picked up the story again, it completely ran away with me. I started and finished within a couple of hours because I simply could not put it down. I loved how some of the secrets were revealed in Evil Among Us, and I also loved the horror and anticipation that the characters such as Seth created and the tensions between some of the younger survivors was creating. It kept the story flowing and also led me closer to what is going to be revealed in The One. It was interesting to also see into another side of Baby and Echo to see that they also harbor human emotion and keep secrets even from their loved ones, and exposing the survivors to Netty's raw emotions I think really helped heal alot of discomfort and rising issues as it made her and Wil and the other elders seem more human to the Hive.<br />There were some sad parts and happy parts and some completely despicable events as well in this one book, but it was so worth the wait and has me waiting very impatiently for book 6 to be released in August. </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Obsession Is A Book - Terrie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Obsession Is A Book - Terrie " href="/user/show/15112957-obsession-is-a-book---terrie">Obsession Is A Book - Terrie </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer624131548" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6188591632864722111">Another fabulous book in the ‘Species Intervention 6609’ series.<br/>Where to start with this one! I’ve read all the previous 4 books and I’m still as gripped as I was with Baby.<br/>Seth, Lorna & Jennifer finally make it to the Hive in this book and their appearance has both a positive and negative effect on the habitants of the Hive, both human and animals.<br/> There is unrest amongst the survivors and this only gets worse. To try and appease them Netty & Wil decide to let them in on some of the plans that </span>
  <span id="freeText6188591632864722111" style="display:none">Another fabulous book in the ‘Species Intervention 6609’ series.<br />Where to start with this one! I’ve read all the previous 4 books and I’m still as gripped as I was with Baby.<br />Seth, Lorna &amp; Jennifer finally make it to the Hive in this book and their appearance has both a positive and negative effect on the habitants of the Hive, both human and animals.<br /> There is unrest amongst the survivors and this only gets worse. To try and appease them Netty &amp; Wil decide to let them in on some of the plans that the Womb has in store. There is a reappearance of other characters which is surprising and not at all suspected.<br />Baby &amp; Echo also have secrets that as always ‘come out in the wash’.<br />It’s hard to think how the author can keep the suspense and angst going while the survivors are all working together to make the best of the situation they find themselves in but suspense and angst there is a plenty. Great writing!<br />The womb is pro-animals and shows much contempt for man &amp; the destruction he weaves. If the womb didn’t need them, I’m in no doubt the survivors would have been left out in the destruction to fend for themselves.<br />There is lots of love, sweat, blood and tears.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6188591632864722111" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6782894031404359294">Evil Among Us (Species Intervention #6609, Book 5) by J.K. Accinni is another great read from this author!<br/><br/>The Earth is in dismal shambles as Seth steers the dying Lorna and Jen toward the Hive. He talks his way in while plotting how to kill Lorna before she can talk. Seth is the evil snake in the garden of Eden. He brings death and chaos to the survivors carefree existence as they care for the rescued wildlife and contemplate the day they can return above ground. Who knew he would unleash the mo</span>
  <span id="freeText6782894031404359294" style="display:none">Evil Among Us (Species Intervention #6609, Book 5) by J.K. Accinni is another great read from this author!<br /><br />The Earth is in dismal shambles as Seth steers the dying Lorna and Jen toward the Hive. He talks his way in while plotting how to kill Lorna before she can talk. Seth is the evil snake in the garden of Eden. He brings death and chaos to the survivors carefree existence as they care for the rescued wildlife and contemplate the day they can return above ground. Who knew he would unleash the monstrous Kreyven. A force for evil? Or Good? I love the use of Toby the elephant who plays such a big part in Bonnie's life. The animals aren't just there. <br /><br />They are integral to the story. And of course, Ceaser the wondrous tiger that guards Scotty. O is her really guarding Chloe? I saw a reference to "her" when The One was feeding Ceasar water. Is that a typo or a clue?? <br /><br />This book in the series moves very quickly from one blind side and heart thumping scene to the another. I refused to put it down. I think you will too.<br /><br />5 stars for this awesome read J.K. Accinni!</span>

  <span id="freeText260304275676819934" style="display:none">I know I have rated most of these books a 5, simply because it is so hard to say one is better than the other when I loved reading every single one of them. Yet, this one I think was the best. There was a lot of answers in this book which I think helped with that and while there was still a lot of characters, in this book it worked a lot better than in Armageddon cometh!! Quite simply you see a different side to echo and bay but at the same time a side that most of us would probably consider abhorrent but at the same time understandable in the circumstances.<br />The story flowed well, the writing was fabulous and the characters all developed into what normal humans are, complete chaos and bedlam. That is why although it has the same amount of stars, I loved this book better than the others.<br />Cannot recommend this book, and the series enough!!   <span id="freeText8488127268462076847" style="display:none">This is already book 5 in the series, and almost the last one. The way the life in the Hive is described, with all the conflicts and solutions, makes this a real pageturner. You get really thrown in the new form of society that is being formed, with the few last humans that survived the destruction of life on earth like we know it. As with all places were people live closely together, of course you get problems among them that have to be solved. Some in a peaceful way, others not that peaceful, in the style of the series.<br /><br />Even though some of the open questions from the earlier books get answered, there are still a lot of questions that stay open. It will be great to read the last book and get an answer to those still. Just hoping it will all fit in the book, as so much is still to come!<br /><br />Waiting now eagerly for the last book to come out!<br /><br /><br />ps. <span id="freeTextContainer15680236279606151538">When I started reading the series, I didn't think I would have fallen for it like I did. Up until Evil Among Us, I had a hard time picking which was my favorite. Now I don't have any doubt that this was my favorite. During the entire read I was on the edge of my seat and couldn't put my book down. I had to find out what was going to happen next. I would love to see this series made into a movie. If it would be, I'd be the first in line to buy it. The entire series is unique and the plot is one t</span>
  <span id="freeText15680236279606151538" style="display:none">When I started reading the series, I didn't think I would have fallen for it like I did. Up until Evil Among Us, I had a hard time picking which was my favorite. Now I don't have any doubt that this was my favorite. During the entire read I was on the edge of my seat and couldn't put my book down. I had to find out what was going to happen next. I would love to see this series made into a movie. If it would be, I'd be the first in line to buy it. The entire series is unique and the plot is one that you wouldn't expect.<br /><br />In Evil Among Us, several characters (Lorna, Jennifer and Seth) struggle to locate the safe haven of the Hive. They come up to several speed bumps along the way, which had my heart racing and I couldn't stop reading. While in the Hive, those who were already there were blessed with the protection from the Womb. This is a fantastic read which I recommend everyone reads. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17899408628982390376">Wow J. K. Accinni has done it again! She has taken me for a whirlwind experience through this book. The twists and turns and bumps in the proverbial road are amazing to say the least. How she comes up with this stuff is beyond me, her imagination is wonderous! This one kind of ties the first 4 books (Baby, Echo, Armegeddon Cometh, and Hive) into one neat little bow and then RIPS is back apart at the end with the whole secret that I am DYING to know from the elders! Good Womb(God) I cannot wait f</span>

The twists and turns and bumps in the proverbial road are amazing to say the least. How she comes up with this stuff is beyond me, her imagination is wonderous! This one kind of ties the first 4 books (Baby, Echo, Armegeddon Cometh, and Hive) into one neat little bow and then RIPS is back apart at the end with the whole secret that I am DYING to know from the elders! Good Womb(God) I cannot wait for the One. Such an amazing story of what Humans could cause our wonderful beautiful world. just amazing! Species Intervention 6609 (how many times our world has had the intervention and been started over again.) is one of THE BEST series I have ever read.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2457449554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1001241975254524396">This is an imaginative writing, and an interesting narrative, but with some serious caveats;<br/>Most of the male characters are psychotic rapist sadists, like if it were something "normal" for everyone in this planet having a dick to be a cruel misogynist. There are some totally unnecessary cruel sadistics scenes. Also, most human women in the series are defendless victims, bordering the imbecility with their inaction, even the mildly "evil" ones.<br/>The whole series is like a vegan-feminist space-soap-</span>
  <span id="freeText1001241975254524396" style="display:none">This is an imaginative writing, and an interesting narrative, but with some serious caveats;<br />Most of the male characters are psychotic rapist sadists, like if it were something "normal" for everyone in this planet having a dick to be a cruel misogynist. There are some totally unnecessary cruel sadistics scenes. Also, most human women in the series are defendless victims, bordering the imbecility with their inaction, even the mildly "evil" ones.<br />The whole series is like a vegan-feminist space-soap-opera with too many religion-like parallels, with the Womb as "God", with the Hive as the Ark, and a private "Hell" with those that misbehaved, and a Heaven in another planet, the aliens physically like a mix of angels and devils, etc. Finally the only ONE printed book saved out of ALL the planet; the "Holy bible".<br />Not to mention the only gay relationship in the series is one of the psychotic male characters, impulsed out of woman rejection.<br />I finally spent much more money in these 6 books than in many others that I read that were either free or just $0.99 that were so much better histories. Way too expensive for such a disappointing agenda.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1001241975254524396" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('66phU0t+ij/x3nA1WNf9mMmPMTosvOay79T4hC2l0+NhdpGHRg+wCixPiot3THRFBh1U7ve1dFZBj8DaPMKONw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WN5LEcKLq1pAWRMKGGUyRnH10nKXoAw6rgHw2zXexcnSArvFz/qRb53I6bQ3/rubvme3pkypnt4AWsiFJLmYHQ==')})
  }
//]]>

After years of enslavement, Netty flees into the night from her rapist and bootlegger husband, traveling back to the farm worked by her parents, where she rescues an unfamiliar damaged creature she finds in a cave in the woods of her childhood, falling in love with the enigmatic alien she names Baby. Together they find happiness and fulfillment despite the changes to Netty\'s body wrought by the proximity of the unusual creature.\n\nDamaged by entry into our atmosphere while pregnant, the confused creature forgets the purpose of his mission, appearing unconcerned with the disappearance of his offspring and savoring the unexpected joy of the love he shares with young Netty.\n\nWhen a handsome Italian stranger comes into Netty\'s life, complications ensue as she falls in love while trying to hide the bizarre and wondrous changes to her farm and her body. Netty, Baby and Wil strive to conquer obstacles thrown in their path by life, succeeding wildly until the heart-rending and astonishingly brutal climax to their story.\n\nThis charming, yet brutal story is the prologue to a series that will chill and surprise you as it foretells the selfishly destructive path man has followed since his species evolved. It pulls no punches while allowing Netty and Baby\'s influence to transcend mortal life as the world dances toward depraved indifference, introducing other characters along the ride that readers will laugh,shed tears with and learn to despise.\n\nWhat lengths will Baby and his offspring go to complete their mission? Will it spell Armageddon for the beleaguered planet with its vulnerable and exploited creatures or will man tip the scales himself, leaving those that love the creatures to salvage the pitiful
